  <h2 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Baobab Privacy Policy</strong></h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp;<em>Last Updated: 5/12/2021</em></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Welcome to Baobab! You are now reading our Privacy Policy, which applies to the virtual reality content viewing applications (each, an “<strong>App</strong>”) made available by Baobab Studios Inc. (“<strong>Baobab</strong>”) and our website located at <a href="http://www.baobabstudios.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">www.baobabstudios.com</span></a> (the “<strong>Site</strong>”). The App, the Site and our related services are collectively called the “Services”. Protecting your privacy is really important to us.&nbsp; With this in mind, we’re providing this Privacy Policy to explains how we collect, use and share information from our about you when you use our Site or Services.&nbsp; This Privacy Policy does not apply to any third-party websites, services or applications, even if they are accessible through our Services or used to access our Services.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><br></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The data controller of your personal information will be Baobab Studios Inc.&nbsp;</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Revisions to this Privacy Policy</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Any information that is collected via our Services is covered by the Privacy Policy in effect at the time such information is collected. We may revise this Privacy Policy from time to time. If we make any material changes to this Privacy Policy, we’ll notify you of those changes by posting them on the Services or by sending you an email or other notification, and we’ll update the “Last Updated Date” above to indicate when those changes will become effective.&nbsp; The date at the top of the Privacy Policy tells you when it was last updated.&nbsp; Any changes to this Privacy Policy will become effective when the revised Privacy Policy is posted.&nbsp; By continuing to use the Site and/or the Services following any changes to this Privacy Policy, you acknowledge you have read and understand the updated Privacy Policy, and you understand that we will collect, use, and share information as stated therein.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">PLEASE READ THIS PRIVACY POLICY CAREFULLY TO UNDERSTAND HOW WE HANDLE YOUR INFORMATION. BY USING THE SERVICES, YOU ACKNOWLEDGE YOU HAVE READ AND UNDERSTAND THE PRIVACY POLICY AND THAT WE WILL COLLECT, USE AND SHARE YOUR INFORMATION AS SET FORTH BELOW.</p><h3 Depending on the partnership, we may share certain information including contact information (at your direction), identification and demographic information, transactional information, user-generated content that you provide, research and feedback, device information and identifiers, connection and usage information, public and commercial information, and social media information.</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong><em>Social Networks</em></strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We may share your information with social media platforms for example, if you click on a Facebook “like” button on a Baobab Service, the “like” may appear on your Facebook account. To control this sharing of information, please review and adjust your privacy settings for the relevant social network.&nbsp; Depending on your privacy settings and actions on such network, we may share contact information, identification and demographic information, user-generated content, device information and identifiers, connection and usage data, and social media information.</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong><em>Analytics</em></strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>We utilize Google Analytics, a service provided by Google, Inc. that we use to gather information about how users engage with our Site and Services. We may disclose any information about you as we, in our sole discretion, believe necessary or appropriate: (i) to respond to claims, legal process (including subpoenas) or other requests from government or other authorities; (ii) to protect our property, rights and safety and the property, rights and safety of a third party or the public in general; (iii) to protect against possible fraud or other illegal activities; or (iv) to stop any activity that we consider illegal, unethical or legally actionable activity.</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong><em>Business Transactions</em></strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Information that we collect from our users, including PII, is considered to be a business asset. Thus, if we are involved in a transaction such as a merger, acquisition, asset sale, transfer of control, bankruptcy, reorganization or sale of assets or diligence associated with such matters, some or all of our assets, including your PII, may be disclosed or transferred to a third party acquirer in connection with the transaction.</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Third Parties:&nbsp;</strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We may share information about how you use the Services and interact with content to better tailor how our Services interact with third-party services, including third-party platforms. To enable these purposes, we may share certain demographics information, user-generated content, device information and identifiers, connection and usage data, geolocation data, public and commercial information, and social media information. These third parties may use their own tracking technologies to collect or request information about you, please see our Cookie Notice.&nbsp; We do not share this information with third party advertisers or advertising networks.</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong><em>Search Engines</em></strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Depending on the Service, you may be able to engage with other members of the Service or the public. We may aggregate or deidentify your information and may use, share, rent or sell aggregated or deidentified information for any purpose, and such information is not subject to this Privacy Policy.</em></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We may share information about you along with a hashed or masked identifier, with third parties so they may better personalize your experience with them and the offers they send you. With your appropriate consent <em>when</em> required, and consistent with applicable law, we may share your video viewing behavior with third parties including service providers, advertising companies, analytic partners, and social media sites.</p></li></ul><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Legal Bases for Use of Your Information</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The laws of some jurisdictions, such as the European Union, require companies to tell you about the legal basis for using, sharing, or disclosing your information. To the extent those laws apply, we may rely on the following legal bases:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Performance of a contract:</strong>&nbsp;where use of your information is necessary to provide you with our Services under a contract, for example the Terms of Service.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Legitimate interest:</strong>&nbsp;where use of your information is necessary for our or others legitimate interests and where the use is not outweighed by your rights and interests. Below are some examples of such interests:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">providing the Services</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">improving our Services and developing new ones</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">recognizing and better understanding our users, including across platforms</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">conducting security and fraud prevention activities</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">marketing and promoting our content and services</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">building and managing business relationships</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">conducting compliance and risk management activities</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">providing and managing access to our systems</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">protecting our rights and assets</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">preventing fraud and other illegal activity</p></li></ul></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Legal obligation:</strong>&nbsp; where use of your information is necessary to comply with laws and regulations such as those relating to anti-bribery and corruption and anti-money-laundering, complying with requests from government bodies or courts, or responding to litigation.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>With consent:</strong>&nbsp; we may ask for your consent to process your information in a certain way.&nbsp; Where we rely on this basis, you have the right to withdraw your consent at any time – please see the <a href="https://www.nbcuniversal.com/privacy?brandA=Focus_Features&amp;intake=Focus_Features#accordionheader5">Your Rights</a> and <a href="https://www.nbcuniversal.com/privacy?brandA=Focus_Features&amp;intake=Focus_Features#accordionheader6">Your Choices</a>&nbsp;sections below to do this.</p></li></ul><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Your Choices</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you want us to delete your PII, please stop using our Services (including uninstalling our App) and stop accessing our Site and contact us at info@baobabvr.com with your request. We’ll take steps to delete your information as soon we can, but some information may remain in archived/backup copies for our records or as otherwise required by law.</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Your Rights</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Depending on where you live, you may have certain rights with respect to your information. For example, under local laws, including in the European Union, you may be able to ask us to:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">provide access to certain information we hold about you, in some cases in a portable format, if technically feasible</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">update or correct your information</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">delete certain information</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">restrict the use of your information</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We will respond within the time period prescribed by applicable law. Please note that many of the above rights are subject to exceptions and limitations.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Some Services can only be provided if we have your information, therefore deletion of your information will result in termination of such Services. &nbsp;&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We will take reasonable steps to verify your identity, including authenticating you through the email address. We may require further documentation such as a password and user ID before granting access to your information.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">California residents with rights under the CCPA or their authorized agents may email <a href="mailto:info@baobabvr.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a> or call [NUMBER] to request access to stored information or deletion of such information.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">U.S. residents who wish to learn more about access or deletion requests may email <a href="mailto:info@baobab.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a>.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you are based outside the U.S. and would like to exercise any individual right you may have please contact us at <a href="mailto:info@baobab.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a><span style="text-decoration:underline"><strong>.</strong></span>&nbsp; Please include “My Rights” in the subject line and provide a clear explanation of which right you are exercising and your country of residence in the body of the email.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Your rights and our responses will vary based on your state or country of residency. Please note that you may be located in a jurisdiction where we are not obligated, or are unable, to fulfill a request.&nbsp; In such a case, your request may not be fulfilled.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you have any unresolved concerns, you may have the right to complain to your local data protection authority.</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">“Do Not Sell My Personal Information” (California Residents only)</h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">California law broadly defines “sale” in a way that may include allowing third parties to receive certain information such as cookies, IP address and/or browsing behavior to add to a profile about your device, browser, or you. We do not currently share your personal information to third parties for advertising purposes.&nbsp; If we modify our privacy policy or practices and begin to sell your personal information, we will provide a means for California residents to opt out of the “sale” of their personal information.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Third Parties’ List – Shine the Light (California Residents only)</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">California residents can also request a list of all the third parties to which we have disclosed certain personal information (as defined by California’s Shine the Light law) during the preceding year for those third parties’ direct marketing purposes. California residents may contact us at <a href="mailto:info@baobab.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a>. In the body of your request, you must include: “California Shine the Light Request”, your name, a current California address including, street address, city, state, and zip code, as well as sufficient information for us to determine if the law applies to you. You will need to attest to the fact that you are a California resident. We will not accept requests by telephone, email, or facsimile, and we are not responsible for notices that are not labeled or sent properly, or that do not have complete information.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Nevada Residents</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We do not engage in the following activity, however Nevada law requires us to post the following: certain Nevada consumers may opt out of the sale of “covered information” for monetary consideration to a person for that person to license or sell such information.&nbsp; “Covered information” includes first and last name, address, email address, phone number, Social Security Number, or an identifier that allows a specific person to be contacted either physically or online.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you are a Nevada resident who has purchased goods or services from us, you may submit a request to opt out of any potential future sales under Nevada law by emailing us at <a href="mailto:info@baobab.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a>.&nbsp; Please use “Nevada Do Not Sell” in the subject line. Note we will take reasonable steps to verify your identity and the authenticity of the request.&nbsp; Once verified, we will maintain your request in the event our practices change. &nbsp;</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Cookies and Similar Technologies</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We and our service providers, advertisers, and other third parties use cookies and similar technologies (e.g., HTTP cookies, HTML 5, flash local storage cookies, web beacons, GIFs, embedded scripts, ETags/cache browsers, and software development kits) to recognize you on, off, and across our Services and your devices. For more information about the use of cookies and similar technologies on the our Services (including your opt-out choices) please see our [LINK <a href="https://www.nbcuniversal.com/privacy/cookies"><span style="text-decoration:underline"><strong>Cookie Notice</strong></span></a>]. &nbsp;</p><h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Mobile App and Connected Devices</strong></h3><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Depending on the device you use, you may be able to manage your advertising and location preferences through your device settings and as outlined in our [LINK <a href="https://www.nbcuniversal.com/privacy/cookies"><span style="text-decoration:underline"><strong>Cookie Notice</strong></span></a>].&nbsp; Many operating systems provide their own instructions on how to prevent the delivery of tailored in-application advertisements. We do not control how the applicable platform operator allows you to manage personalized in-application advertisements. You should review your device manufacturer’s support materials and/or the device settings for the respective operating systems for more detail on how to manage such preferences.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">You can stop all collection of information by a mobile app by uninstalling the app.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>The Security of Your Information</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We take reasonable&nbsp;administrative, technical, physical and electronic measures designed to protect&nbsp;the information that we collect from or about you (including your PII) from unauthorized access, use or disclosure. Please be aware, however, that no method of transmitting information over the Internet or storing information is completely secure. Accordingly, we cannot guarantee the absolute security of any information.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>HOW LONG WE KEEP YOUR INFORMATION</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We will keep your information only for as long as it is necessary to fulfill the purposes described above, unless a longer retention is required or permitted by law. We may delete or de-identify your information sooner if we receive a verifiable deletion request, subject to exemptions under applicable law. The retention period that applies to your information may vary depending on the Services you use and how you interact with them.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Links to Other Sites</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Our Services may contain links to or be accessible through websites and services that are owned or operated by third parties (each, a “Third-Party Service”). Any information that you provide on or to a Third-Party Service or that is collected by a Third-Party Service is provided directly to the owner or operator of the Third-Party Service and is subject to the owner’s or operator’s privacy policy. We’re not responsible for the content, privacy or security practices and policies of any Third-Party Service. To protect your information we recommend that you carefully review the privacy policies of all Third-party Services that you access.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>International Transfer</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We provide Services globally and our company has its headquarters in the United States. We may transfer your information to Related Companies, service providers, and other third parties located outside of your country of residence, including in the United States. This is necessary to provide our Services and for the purposes outlined in this Privacy Policy. &nbsp;Data privacy laws vary from country to country and may not be equivalent to, or as protective as, the laws in your home country.&nbsp; We take steps to ensure that reasonable safeguards are in place with aim to ensure an appropriate level of protection for your information, in accordance with applicable law. These measures include data transfer agreements. By providing us with your information, you acknowledge any such transfer, storage or use.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Our Policy Toward Children</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Our Services are not directed to children under 13 and we do not knowingly collect PII from children under 13. If we learn that we have collected PII of a child under 13 we will take steps to delete such information from our files as soon as possible.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Questions?</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you have any questions about our Privacy Policy, please contact us at: <a href="mailto:info@baobabvr.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">info@baobabvr.com</span></a>.</p>

        const sectionBackground = firstSection ? firstSection.querySelector('.section-background') : null;
        const headerHeight = header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().height : 0;
        const firstSectionHasBackground = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('has-background') >= 0 : false;
        const isFirstSectionInset = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('background-width--inset') >= 0 : false;
        const isLayoutEngineSection = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('layout-engine-section') >= 0 : false;

        if (firstSection) {
          firstSection.style.paddingTop = headerHeight + 'px';
        }
        if (sectionBackground && isLayoutEngineSection) {
          if (isFirstSectionInset) {
            sectionBackground.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
          } else {
            sectionBackground.style.top = '';
          }
        }
        //# sourceURL=headerPositioning.js
      </script>
